by Slate</a></li>\n        </ul>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"page-wrapper\">\n      <div class=\"dark-box\"></div>\n      <div class=\"content\">\n        <div name=\"introduction\" data-unique=\"introduction\"></div><h1 id=\"introduction\">Introduction</h1>\n\n<p>This is the reference documentation for the Mendeley API.  It contains details of the endpoints that the API offers, and examples of how to use it.</p>\n\n<p>For more information, see the <a href=\"http://dev.mendeley.com\">developer portal</a>.</p>\n\n<p>When working with collections, paged results and ordering please consult the <a href=\"http://dev.mendeley.com/reference/topics/pagination.html\">pagination section on our developer portal</a></p>\n\n          <div name=\"annotations\" data-unique=\"annotations\"></div><h1 id=\"annotations\">Annotations</h1>\n\n<div name=\"annotation-attributes\" data-unique=\"annotation-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"annotation-attributes\">Annotation attributes</h2>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>identifier (UUID)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>created</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>date the annotation was created.  This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>last_modified</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>date the annotation was updated. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>color</td>\n<td>color</td>\n<td>RGB values</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>text</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>text value of the annotation</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>positions</td>\n<td>array of HighlightBox’s</td>\n<td>wrapper object contains page and coordinates of the annotation bounding box.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>privacy_level</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>public, group or private.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>document_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>UUID of the document which the file is attached to.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>profile_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>UUID of the user that created the annotation.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>filehash</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>filehash of which the annotation belongs to.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-annotations\" data-unique=\"retrieving-annotations\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-annotations\">Retrieving annotations</h2>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span class=\"s1\">'https://api.mendeley.com/annotations'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Authorization: Bearer &lt;ACCESS_TOKEN&gt;'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Accept: application/vnd.mendeley-annotation.1+json'</span>\n\n<span class=\"o\">{</span>\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"id\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"d6526d08-22f2-4c1f-b80b-092e6e3df528\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"color\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"r\"</span>: 255,\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"g\"</span>: 255,\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"b\"</span>: 0\n    <span class=\"o\">}</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"text\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"This is a sticky note\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"positions\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">[</span>\n      <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n        <span class=\"s2\">\"top_left\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n          <span class=\"s2\">\"x\"</span>: 269.035,\n          <span class=\"s2\">\"y\"</span>: 695.428\n        <span class=\"o\">}</span>,\n        <span class=\"s2\">\"bottom_right\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n          <span class=\"s2\">\"x\"</span>: 269.035,\n          <span class=\"s2\">\"y\"</span>: 695.428\n        <span class=\"o\">}</span>,\n        <span class=\"s2\">\"page\"</span>: 1\n      <span class=\"o\">}</span>\n    <span class=\"o\">]</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"created\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"2011-10-07T14:19:09.000Z\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"last_modified\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"2011-10-07T14:19:37.000Z\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"privacy_level\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"private\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"filehash\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"bd3293b2-d20c-0d9f-3773-df51a506c7b2\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"document_id\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"2a3f09be-75b0-3bf9-bdbd-838c5e588969\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"profile_id\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"e2cc65ad-5ef2-3838-b934-737fdb3b196d\"</span>\n  <span class=\"o\">}</span>\n\n</code></pre>\n<pre><code class=\"highlight java\"><span class=\"n\">AnnotationList</span> <span class=\"n\">annotationList</span> <span class=\"o\">=</span> <span class=\"n\">sdk</span><span class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"na\">getAnnotations</span><span class=\"o\">();</span>\n<span class=\"n\">List</span><span class=\"o\">&lt;</span><span class=\"n\">Annotation</span><span class=\"o\">&gt;</span> <span class=\"n\">annotations</span> <span class=\"o\">=</span> <span class=\"n\">annotationList</span><span class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"na\">annotations</span><span class=\"o\">;</span>\n<span class=\"n\">Page</span> <span class=\"n\">next</span> <span class=\"o\">=</span> <span class=\"n\">annotationList</span><span class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"na\">next</span><span class=\"o\">;</span>\n</code></pre>\n\n<p>Retrieve all your annotations</p>\n\n<div name=\"http-request\" data-unique=\"http-request\"></div><h3 id=\"http-request\">HTTP Request</h3>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET https://api.mendeley.com/annotations</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"url-parameters\" data-unique=\"url-parameters\"></div><h3 id=\"url-parameters\">URL Parameters</h3>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Parameter</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>group_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>UUID of the group you would like to get the annotations from. This will only return all the annotations in that group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>document_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>UUID of the document you would like to get the annotations from. This will only return the annotations associated with that document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>modified_since</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>returns only documents modified since this timestamp. Should be supplied in ISO 8601 format</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>deleted_since</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>returns only documents deleted since this timestamp. Should be supplied in ISO 8601 format</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>limit</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>the maximum number of items on the page. If not supplied, the default is 20. The largest allowable value is 500</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>marker</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>a marker for the last key in the previous page (automatically generated, here for completeness)</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"returns\" data-unique=\"returns\"></div><h3 id=\"returns\">Returns</h3>\n\n<p>Will return a paginated collection of all private annotations data-unique=\"catalog-documents\"></div><h1 id=\"catalog-documents\">Catalog Documents</h1>\n\n<div name=\"core-catalog-document-attributes\" data-unique=\"core-catalog-document-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"core-catalog-document-attributes\">Core catalog document attributes</h2>\n\n<p>The following attributes are returned by default.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Identifier (UUID) of the document. This identifier is set by the server on create and it cannot be modified.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>title</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Title of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>type</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The type of the document. Supported types: journal, book, generic, book_section, conference_proceedings, working_paper, report, web_page, thesis, magazine_article, statute, patent, newspaper_article, computer_program, hearing, television_broadcast, encyclopedia_article, case, film, bill.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>abstract</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Brief summary of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>source</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Publication outlet, i.e. where the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>year</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>Year in which the document was issued/published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>authors</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of authors of the document, as <a href=\"#people\">person</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>identifiers</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of identifiers available for the document. The supported identifiers are: arxiv, doi, isbn, issn, pmid (PubMed), scopus and ssrn.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>keywords</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>50 each</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>link</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Link to the document’s page on the Mendeley website.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"additional-catalog-document-attributes\" data-unique=\"additional-catalog-document-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"additional-catalog-document-attributes\">Additional catalog document attributes</h2>\n\n<p>The following attributes are available using a <a href=\"#catalog-document-views\">view</a>.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>month</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>Month in which the document was issued/published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>day</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>Day in which the document was issued/published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>revision</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Number identifying the item (e.g. a report number).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>pages</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>range of pages the document covers in the issue, e.g 4-8.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>volume</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>volume holding the document, e.g “2” from journal volume 2.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>issue</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>issue holding the document, e.g. “5” for a journal article from journal volume 2, issue 5</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>websites</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>Where the document was accessed from.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>publisher</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Publisher of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>city</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>city where the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>edition</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>edition holding the document, e.g. “3” from the third edition of a book.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>institution</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Institution in which the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>series</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>title of the collection holding the document (e.g. the series title for a book)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>chapter</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Chapter number.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>editors</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of editors of the document. Like authors, this is a collection (array) of person objects, which include first_name and last_name (strings), as <a href=\"#people\">person</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>file_attached</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>reader_count</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>Total number of users in Mendeley that have the document in their library.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>reader_count_by_academic_status</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>Number of readers based on their academic status.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>reader_count_by_discipline</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>Number of readers based on their discipline.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>reader_count_by_country</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>Number of readers based on their country.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>group_count</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>Number of Mendeley groups that this document has been added to.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>imported</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td>Whether the document metadata has been imported from a source other than a users library. For example, Scopus and is therefore likely to be of a higher quality.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>has_pdf</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td>Whether the catalogue document has an associated full-text pdf suitable for download.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"catalog-document-views\" data-unique=\"catalog-document-views\"></div><h2 id=\"catalog-document-views\">Catalog document views</h2>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Value</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>bib</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus the bibliographic data. This includes: pages, volume, issue, websites, month, publisher, day, city, edition, institution, series, chapter, revision and editors.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>client</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus file_attached and imported.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>stats</td>\n<td>This view will return the core fields plus the statistics data. This includes: reader_count, reader_count_by_academic_status, reader_count_by_discipline, reader_by_country and group_count.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>all</td>\n<td>Will return all fields.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-catalog-documents\" data-unique=\"retrieving-catalog-documents\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-catalog-documents\">Retrieving catalog class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"nb\">list</span><span class=\"p\">()</span>\n\n<span class=\"k\">for</span> <span class=\"n\">doc</span> <span class=\"ow\">in</span> <span class=\"o\">.</span>\n</code></pre>\n\n<p>Retrieve documents which match general query terms.</p>\n\n<div name=\"http-request34\" data-unique=\"http-request34\"></div><h3 id=\"http-request\">HTTP Request</h3>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET https://api.mendeley.com/search/catalog</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"url-parameters35\" data-unique=\"url-parameters35\"></div><h3 id=\"url-parameters\">URL Parameters</h3>\n\n<p>The search query is considered to be a string of terms separated by spaces. The search will return documents which match any of these, but rank those which match many terms higher than those which only match a few.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Parameter</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>query</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Query terms, which match any field in the document, e.g. title, author etc (<strong>required</strong>).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>view</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Request additional fields in the documents returned, as for <a href=\"#catalog-documents\">Catalog Documents</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"advanced-search\" data-unique=\"advanced-search\"></div><h2 id=\"advanced-search\">Advanced fields.</p>\n\n<div name=\"http-request37\" data-unique=\"http-request37\"></div><h3 id=\"http-request\">HTTP Request</h3>\n\n<p>Advanced search uses the same endpoint as search by query:</p>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET https://api.mendeley.com/search/catalog</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"url-parameters38\" data-unique=\"url-parameters38\"></div><h3 id=\"url-parameters\">URL Parameters</h3>\n\n<p>Multiple search fields may be specified. At least one of <code class=\"prettyprint\">title</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">author</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">source</code> or <code class=\"prettyprint\">abstract</code> <strong>must</strong> be provided. If more than one of these is set, the results will return documents which match any of these, but rank those which match several fields higher than those which match fewer fields.</p>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">min_year</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">max_year</code> and <code class=\"prettyprint\">open_access</code> act as filters. Setting either a minimum or maximum year excludes documents which do not have a year defined.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Parameter</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>title</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Matches terms in the title of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>author</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Matches the names of one or more authors.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>source</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Matches the publication name.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>abstract</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Matches terms in the abstract.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>min_year</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>The earliest publication year to return results for.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>max_year</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td>The latest publication year to return results for.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>open_access</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td>Specify true to limit results to open access publications (default = false).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>view</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Request additional fields in documents returned, as for <a href=\"#catalog-documents\">Catalog Documents</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n          <div name=\"datasets\" data-unique=\"datasets\"></div><h1 id=\"datasets\">Datasets</h1>\n\n<div name=\"public-dataset-attributes\" data-unique=\"public-dataset-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"public-dataset-attributes\">Public dataset data-unique=\"draft-dataset-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"draft-dataset-attributes\">Draft dataset attributes</h2>\n\n<p>Draft dataset objects are similar to public dataset objects. They have some additional properties to help manage access to unpublished datasets.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The unique identifier for the dataset (required for other operations).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>name</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The name of the dataset.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>description</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>A description of the data (files) contained in the dataset.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>files</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>The dataset files, as <a href=\"#dataset-file-attributes\">file objects</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>categories</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>The dataset categories, as <a href=\"#category-attributes\">category objects</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>contributors</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>The contributors of the dataset, as <a href=\"#contributor-attributes\">contributor objects</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>doi</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>The DOI associated with the dataset, as <a href=\"#doi-attributes\">DOI object</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>versions</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>All versions of this dataset, as <a href=\"#version-attributes\">version objects</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>data_licence</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>The licence that applies to this dataset version, as <a href=\"#data-licence-attributes\">data licence object</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>articles</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>Journal articles associated with the dataset, <a href=\"#article-attributes\">article objects</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>owner_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>ID of dataset owner</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>created_data</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Date that this dataset was created. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>last_modification_date</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Date that this dataset was last modified. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>access_code</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>This will allow anyone to see the dataset if provided.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>permissions</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>Permission IDs applied to this draft</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"submission-attributes\" data-unique=\"submission-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"submission-attributes\">Submission attributes</h2>\n\n<p>Submissions are a way for submission systems to add datasets (draft) related to the article submissions. Submissions and their data is only available to submission system and the authors associated with it.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The unique (among the submission system) identifier for the submission (submission id) (required for other operations).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>owner</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>Article author information as <a href=\"#owner-attributes\">owner object</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>submission_data</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Submission system specific data in a form of JSON object</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>submission_token</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>A token generated when submission is created. It can later be used by other API clients (on behalf of the journal author) to add, modify and unlink datasets.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>datasets</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>datasets, associated with submission, as objects with “id” and “version” properties of the draft datasets.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"owner-attributes\" data-unique=\"owner-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"owner-attributes\">Owner attributes</h2>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>email</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The article author’s email address.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"specifying-fields-to-return\" data-unique=\"specifying-fields-to-return\"></div><h2 id=\"specifying-fields-to-return\">Specifying fields to return</h2>\n\n<p>By default, only the id will be returned for requests. You should specify which attributes to return using the <code class=\"prettyprint\">fields</code> query paramenter.</p>\n\n<p>For example, to return a list of datasets with the <code class=\"prettyprint\">id</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">version</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">title</code>, <code class=\"prettyprint\">description</code> and the <code class=\"prettyprint\">mime_type</code> for <code class=\"prettyprint\">files</code>, you would provide:</p>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET /datasets?fields=results.id,results.version,results.name,results.description,results.files.mime_type</code></p>\n\n<p>For nested objects such as contributors, you must provide the keys within the object.</p>\n\n<p>For example, to return a list of datasets, each with contributors’ <code class=\"prettyprint\">first_name</code> and <code class=\"prettyprint\">last_name</code> you would provide:</p>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET /datasets?fields=results.contributors.first_name,results.contributors.last_name</code></p>\n\n<p>If you want to receive all fields, you can pass <code class=\"prettyprint\">*</code> to the fields parameter. Be aware that this query may take longer to receive and you may want to avoid using this in production.</p>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">GET /datasets?fields=*</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-datasets-(public)\" data-unique=\"retrieving-datasets-(public)\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-datasets-(public)\">Retrieving datasets (public)</h2>\n\n<div class=\"prettyprint\">GET https://api.mendeley.com/disciplines</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"returns105\" data-unique=\"returns105\"></div><h3 id=\"returns\">Returns</h3>\n\n<p>A 200 OK response containing a all disciplines and subdisciplines in Mendeley.</p>\n\n          <div name=\"documents\" data-unique=\"documents\"></div><h1 id=\"documents\">Documents</h1>\n\n<div name=\"core-document-attributes\" data-unique=\"core-document-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"core-document-attributes\">Core document attributes</h2>\n\n<p>The following attributes are returned by default.</p>\n\n<p>Some string attributes have a maximum length - these are indicated in the table below.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Maximum length</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Identifier (UUID) of the document. This identifier is set by the server on create and it cannot be modified.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>title</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>500</td>\n<td>Title of the document. This is a required field.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>type</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>The type of the document. Supported types: journal, book, generic, book_section, conference_proceedings, working_paper, report, web_page, thesis, magazine_article, statute, patent, newspaper_article, computer_program, hearing, television_broadcast, encyclopedia_article, case, film, bill.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>profile_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Profile id (UUID) of the Mendeley user that added the document to the system.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>group_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Group id (UUID) that the document belongs to.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>created</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Date the document was added to the system. This date is set by the server after a successful create request. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>last_modified</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Date in which the document was last modified. This date is set by the server after a successful update request. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>abstract</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>10,000</td>\n<td>Brief summary of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>source</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Publication outlet, i.e. where the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>year</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Year in which the document was issued/published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>authors</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>List of authors of the document, as <a href=\"#people\">person</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>identifiers</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>500 each</td>\n<td>List of identifiers available for the document. The supported identifiers are: arxiv, doi, isbn, issn, pmid (PubMed), scopus and ssrn.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>keywords</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>300 each</td>\n<td>List of author-supplied keywords for the document.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"additional-document-attributes\" data-unique=\"additional-document-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"additional-document-attributes\">Additional document attributes</h2>\n\n<p>The following attributes are available using a <a href=\"#document-views\">view</a>.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Maximum length</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>month</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Month in which the document was issued/published. This should be an integer between 1 and 12.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>day</td>\n<td>integer</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Day in which the document was issued/published. This should be an integer between 1 and 31.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>revision</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Number identifying the item (e.g. a report number).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>pages</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>50</td>\n<td>range of pages the document covers in the issue, e.g 4-8.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>volume</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>20</td>\n<td>volume holding the document, e.g “2” from journal volume 2.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>issue</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>issue holding the document, e.g. “5” for a journal article from journal volume 2, issue 5</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>websites</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>5000 total</td>\n<td>Where the document was accessed from.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>publisher</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Publisher of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>city</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>city where the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>edition</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>20</td>\n<td>edition holding the document, e.g. “3” from the third edition of a book.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>institution</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Institution in which the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>series</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>title of the collection holding the document (e.g. the series title for a book)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>chapter</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>20</td>\n<td>Chapter number.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>editors</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>List of editors of the document, as <a href=\"#people\">person</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>accessed</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Date that the document was accessed. This date is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>tags</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>100 each</td>\n<td>List of user-supplied tags for the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>read</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag used to identify whether the document has been read or not.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>starred</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag used to identify whether the user has marked the document as favourite.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>authored</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag used to identify whether the user has authored the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>confirmed</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag to identify whether the metadata of the document is correct after it has been extracted from the PDF file.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>hidden</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag to identify whether Mendeley can publish this document to the Mendeley catalog.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>file_attached</td>\n<td>boolean</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>Flag to identify whether the document has a file attached.  Files can be retrieved using the <a href=\"#files\">files API</a>.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>citation_key</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Identifier used by BibTeX when citing documents.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>source_type</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Original type of a document imported from BibTeX.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>language</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Language of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>short_title</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>50</td>\n<td>A short version of the title, used in some citations.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>reprint_edition</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>10</td>\n<td>Edition number of this reprint of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>genre</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Class, type or genre of the document.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>country</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Country where the document was published.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>translators</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td></td>\n<td>List of translators of the document, as <a href=\"#people\">person</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>series_editor</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Editor name for a book series.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>code</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Code for legal documents.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>medium</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Medium description (e.g. “CD”, “DVD”).</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>user_context</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>The format of the item (e.g. Journal)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>department</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>University department name.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>patent_owner</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Name of number.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>patent_legal_status</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Legal status of document, example values “Restricted”, “Pending approval”, “Granted”.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"people\" data-unique=\"people\"></div><h3 id=\"people\">People</h3>\n\n<p>People are represented as an object with the following attributes:</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Maximum length</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>last_name</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>Last name of the person.  Required.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>first_name</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td>First name of the person.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"document-views\" data-unique=\"document-views\"></div><h2 id=\"document-views\">Document views</h2>\n\n<p>To get additional fields, you can use one of the following views:</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Value</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>bib</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus the bibliographic data. This includes: pages, volume, issue, websites, month, publisher, day, city, edition, institution, series, chapter, revision, editors, accessed, citation_key, source_type, language, short_title, reprint_edition, genre, country, translators, series_editor, code, medium, user_context, department.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>client</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus the fields needed for clients to sync across different devices like read, starred, authored, confirmed, hidden and file_attached.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>tags</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus tags.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>patent</td>\n<td>Will return the core fields plus patent_owner, patent_application_number and patent_legal_status.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>all</td>\n<td>Will return all fields.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-a-document\" data-unique=\"retrieving-a-document\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-a-document\">Retrieving a document</h2>\n<pre For example, application/pdf.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Content-Disposition</td>\n<td>This header is used to extract the file’s name. The value should be, for example: attachment; filename=“example.pdf”</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Link</td>\n<td>We use this header to specify the document that the file should be attached to. For example: https://api.mendeley.com/documents/cfb60e27-d3e4-397d-bb59-fc8388b98152</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"returns164\" data-unique=\"returns164\"></div><h3 id=\"returns\">Returns</h3>\n\n<p>A successful request will respond with a 201 Created code and a Location header where you can find the URL where you can download the file.</p>\n\n<div name=\"linking-a-file-content-to-a-file\" data-unique=\"linking-a-file-content-to-a-file\"></div><h2 id=\"linking-a-file-content-to-a-file\">Linking a file content to a file</h2>\n\n<p>Creates a file based on a file content ticket obtained from /file_contents endpoint</p>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span class=\"s1\">'https://api.mendeley.com/files'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-X POST <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Authorization: Bearer &lt;ACCESS_TOKEN&gt;'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Accept: application/vnd.mendeley-file.1+json'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Content-Disposition: attachment; filename=\"file.pdf\"'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Content-Type: application/vnd.mendeley-file-link.1+json'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Link: &lt;https://api.mendeley.com/documents/34542a05-ca31-3f25-9280-678e81a8a848&gt;; rel=\"document\"'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n--data-binary <span class=\"s1\">'{\"file_content_ticket\" : \"&lt;FILE_CONTENT_TICKET_ID&gt;\"}'</span>\n</code></pre>\n\n<div name=\"header-parameters166\" data-unique=\"header-parameters166\"></div><h3 id=\"header-parameters\">Header Parameters</h3>\n\n<p>The following header parameters must be set.</p>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Parameter</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>Accept</td>\n<td>application/vnd.mendeley-file.1+json</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Content-Type</td>\n<td>application/vnd.mendeley-file-link.1+json</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Content-Disposition</td>\n<td>This header is used to extract the file’s name. The value should be, for example: attachment; filename=“example.pdf”</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Link</td>\n<td>We use this header to specify the document that the file should be attached to. For example: https://api.mendeley.com/documents/cfb60e27-d3e4-397d-bb59-fc8388b98152</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"returns167\" data-unique=\"returns167\"></div><h3 id=\"returns\">Returns</h3>\n\n<p>A successful request will respond with a 201 Created code and a Location header where you can find the URL where you can download the file.</p>\n\n<div name=\"deleting-a-file\" data-unique=\"deleting-a-file\"></div><h2 id=\"deleting-a-file\">Deleting a file</h2>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span class=\"s1\">'https://api.mendeley.com/files/16bd4f6e-4578-3391-356d-66b374143457'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-X DELETE <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Authorization: Bearer &lt;ACCESS_TOKEN&gt;'</span>\n</code></pre>\n<pre><code class=\"highlight python\"><span class=\"nb\">file</span><span class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"n\">delete</span><span class=\"p\">()</span>\n</code></pre>\n<pre><code class=\"highlight java\"><span class=\"n\">DeleteFileCallback</span> <span class=\"n\">deleteFileCallback</span> <span class=\"o\">=</span> <span class=\"k\">new</span> <span class=\"n\">DeleteFileCallback</span><span class=\"o\">()</span> <span class=\"o\">{</span> <span class=\"o\">...</span> <span class=\"o\">}</span>\n<span class=\"n\">asyncSdk</span><span class=\"o\">.</span><span class=\"na\">deleteFile</span><span class=\"o\">(</span><span class=\"s\">\"16bd4f6e-4578-3391-356d-66b374143457\"</span><span class=\"o\">,</span> <span class=\"n\">deleteFileCallback</span><span class=\"o\">);</span>\n</code></pre>\n\n<p>Deletes a file.</p>\n\n<div name=\"http-request169\" data-unique=\"http-request169\"></div><h3 id=\"http-request\">HTTP Request</h3>\n\n<p><code class=\"prettyprint\">DELETE /files/{id}</code></p>\n\n<div name=\"returns170\" data-unique=\"returns170\"></div><h3 id=\"returns\">Returns</h3>\n\n<p>A successful request will respond with a 204 No Content code.     <div name=\"groups\" data-unique=\"groups\"></div><h1 id=\"groups\">Groups</h1>\n\n<div name=\"group-attributes\" data-unique=\"group-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"group-attributes\">Group attributes</h2>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Identifier (UUID) of the group. This identifier is set by the server on create and cannot be modified.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>link</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>URL of the group page in Mendeley.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>owning_profile_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Profile identifier of the owner of the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>access_level</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Whether the group is public, private or invite_only. More on access levels below.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>created</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Date the group was created. This date is set by the server after a successful create reques and is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>name</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The name of the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>description</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Small description of what the group is about.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>photo</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>The photo object contains the URL to the photo/logo of the group. There are three sizes available: original, standard and square.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>webpage</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Website of the group outside Mendeley.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>disciplines</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of disciplines the group is part of.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>tags</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of tags assigned to the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>role</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Role of the authenticated user in the group. More on group roles below.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"group-roles\" data-unique=\"group-roles\"></div><h3 id=\"group-roles\">Group roles</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li><strong>owner</strong>: the creator of the group.</li>\n<li><strong>admin</strong>: administrator of the group. Only owners and admins can make other members administrators.</li>\n<li><strong>normal</strong>: normal member of the group. Users can add new references, add files and start discussions in the newsfeed of the group.</li>\n<li><strong>follower</strong>: followers of the group. Only public groups can have followers. Followers cannot interact with other members, i.e. post in newsfeed and participate in discussions, nor add references to the group. This is a read-only access membership.</li>\n<li><strong>invited</strong>: person who has been invited to the group, but not accepted the invitation.  This is a read-only access membership.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-groups\" data-unique=\"retrieving-groups\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-groups\">Retrieving groups</h2>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span class=\"s1\">'https://api.mendeley.com/groups'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Authorization: Bearer &lt;ACCESS_TOKEN&gt;'</span> <span class=\"se\">\\</span>\n-H <span class=\"s1\">'Accept: application/vnd.mendeley-group.1+json'</span>\n\n<span class=\"o\">[</span>\n  <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"name\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"Mendeley Advisor Group\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"description\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"This is an invite-only communication channel for Mendeley Advisors. Meet your fellow advisors from around the world, share papers, presentations, tips, and let us know how we're doing.  Also feel free to post your upcoming presentation to the </span><span class=\"se\">\\\"</span><span class=\"s2\">Events Page</span><span class=\"se\">\\\"</span><span class=\"s2\"> by adding it here: www.mendeley.com/events. Add tips, tricks, and any relevant updates to the Mendeley Resource Center: http://resources.mendeley.com/\"</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"disciplines\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">[</span>\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"Computer and Information Science\"</span>,\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"Social Sciences\"</span>,\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"Design\"</span>\n    <span class=\"o\">]</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"tags\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">[]</span>,\n    <span class=\"s2\">\"photo\"</span>: <span class=\"o\">{</span>\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"original\"</span>: <span class=\"s2\">\"http://s3.amazonaws.com/mendeley-photos/bc/e8/bce8c532283273fb0f511321adcc2cafd07f5876.png\"</span>,\n      <span class=\"s2\">\"standard\"</span>: <span Parameters</h3>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Parameter</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>limit</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>the maximum number of items on the This identifier is set by the server on create and cannot be modified.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>link</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>URL of the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>owning_profile_id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Profile identifier of the owner of the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>access_level</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Whether the group is public, private or invite_only. More on access levels below.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>created</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Date the group was created. This date is set by the server after a successful create request and is represented in ISO 8601 format.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>name</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>The name of the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>description</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Small description of what the group is about.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>photo</td>\n<td>object</td>\n<td>The photo object contains the URL to the photo/logo of the group. There are three sizes available: original, standard and square.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>webpage</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Website of the group outside Mendeley.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>disciplines</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of disciplines the group is part of.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>tags</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of tags assigned to the group.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>role</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Role of the authenticated user in the group. More on group roles below.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"group-roles249\" data-unique=\"group-roles249\"></div><h3 id=\"group-roles\">Group roles</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li><strong>owner</strong>: owner of the group.</li>\n<li><strong>admin</strong>: administrator of the group. Only owners and admins can make other members administrators.</li>\n<li><strong>normal</strong>: normal member of the group. Users can add new references, add files and start discussions in the newsfeed of the group.</li>\n<li><strong>follower</strong>: followers of the group. Only public and invite-only groups can have followers. Followers cannot interact with other members, i.e. post in newsfeed and participate in discussions, nor add references to the group. This is a read-only access membership.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div name=\"group-types\" data-unique=\"group-types\"></div><h3 id=\"group-types\">Group types</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li><strong>private</strong>: publically not visible, users can’t join nor follow, they have to be invited.</li>\n<li><strong>invite_only</strong>: publically visible, users can’t join, can follow, can ask to join.</li>\n<li><strong>public</strong>: publically visible, user can join or follow.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div name=\"creating-group\" data-unique=\"creating-group\"></div><h2 containing a all identifier types. </p>\n\n          <div name=\"institution-trees\" data-unique=\"institution-trees\"></div><h1 id=\"institution-trees\">Institution Trees</h1>\n\n<p>An institution tree is a set of institutions that form a hierarchy, connected by the parent_id attribute, eg. Cambridge University -&gt; University of Cambridge Pembroke College etc. \nThe id field within the response indicates the root institution.   An institution tree may be either partial or complete.  Partial infers that the root institution may have a parent, \nwhereas complete is where the root institution has no parent.</p>\n\n<div name=\"institution-tree-attributes\" data-unique=\"institution-tree-attributes\"></div><h2 id=\"institution-tree-attributes\">Institution tree attributes</h2>\n\n<table><thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Attribute</th>\n<th>Type</th>\n<th>Description</th>\n</tr>\n</thead><tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>id</td>\n<td>string</td>\n<td>Identifier (UUID) of the root institution.  This should be used by tree walking algorithms, eg. to build the tree.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>institution_nodes</td>\n<td>array</td>\n<td>List of institutions as <a href=\"#institutions\">institution</a> objects.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n<div name=\"retrieving-complete-institution_trees\" data-unique=\"retrieving-complete-institution_trees\"></div><h2 id=\"retrieving-complete-institution_trees\">Retrieving complete institution_trees</h2>\n\n<p>This institution_id parameter may be any institution within the returned tree, eg. it could be a leaf node.</p>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span institutions by hint</h2>\n\n<ul>\n<li><p>Hint must be at least three characters in length.</p></li>\n<li><p>Limited to 100 results.  If no limit is provided then up to 100 results will be returned.</p></li>\n<li><p>Ordering of results is primarily based upon size of institution in terms of person count.</p></li>\n<li><p>Name and alternative names are searched when retrieving by hint.</p></li>\n<li><p>Hint is case insensitive.</p></li>\n</ul>\n<pre style=\"display: block;\"><code class=\"highlight shell\">curl <span The newly created resource can be referenced by the URI(s) returned in the Location header.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>204</td>\n<td>No content – The request was successful and no extra information will be provided in the body of the response.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>400</td>\n<td>Bad Request – The request you sent to the server is invalid.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>401</td>\n<td>Unauthorized – Your API key is wrong</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>403</td>\n<td>Forbidden – Access to the resource is not allowed.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>404</td>\n<td>Not Found – The resource you were requesting cannot be found.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>405</td>\n<td>Method Not Allowed – The HTTP method (GET/POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE) is not valid for this resource.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>406</td>\n<td>Not Acceptable – The media type in the Accept header is not valid for this resource.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>409</td>\n<td>Conflict – The resource conflicts with one that already exists.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>412</td>\n<td>Precondition Failed</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>415</td>\n<td>Unsupported Media Type – The media type in the Content-Type header is not valid for this resource.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>422</td>\n<td>Unprocessable Entity – The server understands the request entity but was semantically erroneous. See <a href=\"http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4918\">RFC-4918</a></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>429</td>\n<td>Too Many Requests - We’ve rate limited you. Contact api-support@mendeley.com.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>500</td>\n<td>Internal Server Error – We had a problem with our server. Try again later.</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>503</td>\n<td>Service Unavailable – We’re temporarily offline for maintenance. Please try again later.</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table>\n\n      </div>\n      <div class=\"dark-box\">\n          <div class=\"lang-selector\">\n                <a href=\"#\" data-language-name=\"shell\" class=\"active\">cURL</a>\n          </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  <script defer=\"\" src=\"https://static.cloudflareinsights.com/beacon.min.js/v4513226cdae34746b4dedf0b4dfa099e1781791509496\" integrity=\"sha512-ZE9pZaUXND66v380QUtch/5sE9tPFh2zg45pR2PB0CVkCtOREv2AJKkSidISWkysEuQ0EH8faUU5du78bx87UQ==\" data-cf-beacon=\"{&quot;version&quot;:&quot;2024.11.0&quot;,&quot;token&quot;:&quot;84e449ada9f2403eb49fdc7135afd6e1&quot;,&quot;server_timing&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:{&quot;cfCacheStatus&quot;:true,&quot;cfEdge&quot;:true,&quot;cfExtPri&quot;:true,&quot;cfL4&quot;:true,&quot;cfOrigin&quot;:true,&quot;cfSpeedBrain&quot;:true},&quot;location_startswith&quot;:null}}\" crossorigin=\"anonymous\"></script>\n\n\n</body></html>",
